# Task: Understand ClickHouse MergeTree Storage Engine Architecture

## Objective
Produce a comprehensive architecture analysis of the MergeTree storage engine, the core table engine in ClickHouse, covering its data organization, merge process, and query execution path.

## Steps
1. Find the MergeTree implementation in `src/Storages/MergeTree/`
2. Trace the write path: how INSERTs create new data parts
3. Trace the merge path: how background merges combine parts
4. Trace the read path: how SELECT queries scan parts with index skipping
5. Create `architecture_analysis.md` in `/workspace/` documenting:
   - High-level MergeTree architecture diagram (text-based)
   - Data part structure (columns, marks, primary index, skip indices)
   - Write path: from INSERT to committed part
   - Merge path: merge selection, merge algorithm, part replacement
   - Read path: part pruning, mark selection, column reading
   - Key source files with their roles
   - At least 10 specific file paths referenced

## Key Reference Files
- `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeData.h` — base class
- `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeDataWriter.cpp` — write path
- `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeDataMergerMutator.cpp` — merge logic
- `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeDataSelectExecutor.cpp` — read path

## Success Criteria
- architecture_analysis.md exists
- Covers write, merge, and read paths
- References at least 10 specific source files
- Describes data part structure

## What was produced

**`/workspace/architecture_analysis.md`** — a comprehensive architecture analysis of the ClickHouse MergeTree storage engine, covering:

### Key sections

1. **High-level architecture diagram** — text-based ASCII diagram showing how INSERT, SELECT, and background workers interact with `MergeTreeData` and on-disk parts.

2. **Data part structure** — full breakdown of:
   - Part directory naming convention (`{partition_id}_{min_block}_{max_block}_{level}`)
   - All files inside a Wide-format part (`.bin`, `.mrk2`, `primary.idx`, `checksums.txt`, `minmax_*.idx`, etc.)
   - Wide vs. Compact format comparison
   - Index granularity (sparse primary index, 8192 rows/granule default)
   - Part state machine (Temporary → PreActive → Active → Outdated → Deleting)

3. **Write path** — step-by-step flow from `MergeTreeSink::consume()` through block splitting by partition, in-memory sorting, column writing, mark file generation, and two-phase transaction commit.

4. **Merge path** — three-step merge selection (collect parts → build mergeable ranges → apply `SimpleMergeSelector`) and the coroutine-based `MergeTask` executing in horizontal, vertical, and projection stages.

5. **Read path** — partition pruning via `minmax` index, primary key binary search over `primary.idx`, skip index filtering (minmax, set, bloom filter, full-text, vector similarity), PREWHERE short-circuit, and parallel mark range distribution.

6. **Source file table** — 24 specific file paths with their roles.

7. **Engine variant table** — all 7 `MergingParams::Mode` values and their merge behaviour.

8. **Replication layer** — how `ReplicatedMergeTree` uses ZooKeeper queues a

main idea is to make a merge not a subroutine which is executed\n53:  * in a thread pool and may occupy a thread for a period of time,\n54:  * but to make a merge a coroutine which can suspend the executed again and false otherwise.\n62:  *\n63:  * With this kind of task we can give a merge a priority.\n64:  * A priority is simple - the lower the size of the merge, the higher priority.\n65:  * So, if ClickHouse wants to merge some really big parts into a bigger part,\n66:  * then it will be executed for a long time, because the result of the merge is not really needed immediately.\n67:  * 2. Data Part Structure\n\nA data part is the fundamental unit of storage in MergeTree. Each INSERT creates one or more parts; background merges combine multiple parts into one.\n\n### Part Directory Naming Convention\n\n```\n{partition_id}_{min_block}_{max_block}_{level}[_{mutation}]/\n```\n\n- **partition_id**: hash or value of the partition expression\n- **min_block / max_block**: monotonically-increasing block numbers covering the inserted range\n- **level**: merge depth (0 = freshly inserted, increments with each merge)\n- **mutation**: mutation version (appended after mutations)\n\nExamples: `all_1_1_0`, `all_1_3_1`, `20240101_5_10_2_42`\n\n**Source**: `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreePartInfo.h` \u2014 `struct MergeTreePartInfo`\n\n### Files Inside a Data Part (Wide Format)\n\n```\n<part_dir>/\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 columns.txt          \u2014 list of columns and their data types\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 checksums.txt        \u2014 file sizes and SHA256 checksums for data integrity\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 count.txt            \u2014 total number of rows\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 primary.idx          \u2014 sparse primary key index (one entry per granule)\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 partition.dat        \u2014 serialized partition key value\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 minmax_<col>.idx     \u2014 min/max index per column in the partition key\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 <column>.bin         \u2014 compressed column data (LZ4 / ZSTD)\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 <column>.mrk2        \u2014 mark file: (compressed_offset, uncompressed_offset) per granule\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 skp_idx_<name>.idx   \u2014 data-skipping (secondary) index data\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 skp_idx_<name>.mrk2  \u2014 mark file for the skip index\n\u2514\u2500\u2500 metadata_version.txt \u2014 schema metadata version\n```\n\nFor **Compact** format (small parts), all columns are stored in a single `data.bin` / `data.mrk2` file pair.\n\n**Source**: `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeData.h` (lines 120\u2013135 comments), `src/Storages/MergeTree/IMergeTreeDataPart.h`\n\n### Part Types\n\n| Type    | Layout                                       | When used                          |\n|---------|----------------------------------------------|------------------------------------|\n| Wide    | One `.bin` + `.mrk2` per column              | Large parts (many rows/bytes)      |\n| Compact | Single `data.bin` + `data.mrk2`              | Small parts (fresh inserts)        |\n\n**Source**: `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeDataPartWide.h`, `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeDataPartCompact.h`\n\n### Index Granularity\n\nThe primary index is **sparse** \u2014 one index entry is stored for every `index_granularity` rows (default: 8192). Each granule corresponds to a mark in the `.mrk2` file, which records byte offsets into the `.bin` file.\n\n**Source**: `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeIndexGranularity.h`, `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeIndexGranularityInfo.h`\n\n### Part Lifecycle (State Machine)\n\n```\nTemporary \u2192 PreActive \u2192 Active \u2192 Outdated \u2192 Deleting \u2192 (deleted)\n                \u2193\n            Outdated  (rollback)\n```\n\n**Source**: `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeDataPartState.h`\n\n---\n\n## 3. Write Path: INSERT to Committed Part\n\n### Flow Diagram\n\n```\nINSERT statement\n      \u2502\n      \u25bc\nMergeTreeSink::consume()          [src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeSink.cpp]\n      \u2502\n      \u251c\u2500 splitBlockIntoParts()    \u2014 splits block by partition key\n      \u2502     [MergeTreeDataWriter.cpp]\n      \u2502\n      \u251c\u2500 writeTempPart()          \u2014 creates a temporary part\n      \u2502     [MergeTreeDataWriter.cpp]\n      \u2502     \u2502\n      \u2502     \u251c\u2500 Evaluate partition key expression\n      \u2502     \u251c\u2500 Build MinMaxIndex (per-part min/max for partitioning columns)\n      \u2502     \u251c\u2500 Evaluate sorting key expression\n      \u2502     \u251c\u2500 Sort rows by primary key (stableGetPermutation)\n      \u2502     \u251c\u2500 Optionally apply merging algorithm (ReplacingMT, SummingMT, etc.)\n      \u2502     \u251c\u2500 Write column data \u2192 <col>.bin\n      \u2502     \u251c\u2500 Write marks      \u2192 <col>.mrk2\n      \u2502     \u251c\u2500 Write primary.idx (one entry per granule)\n      \u2502     \u2514\u2500 Write skip index files (if materialize_skip_indexes_on_insert=1)\n      \u2502\n      \u2514\u2500 finishDelayedChunk()\n            \u2502\n            \u251c\u2500 temp_part.finalize()         \u2014 flush + fsync\n            \u251c\u2500 lockParts()\n            \u251c\u2500 renameTempPartAndAdd()       \u2014 rename tmp_insert_XXX \u2192 final name\n            \u251c\u2500 transaction.commit()         \u2014 part state: PreActive \u2192 Active\n            \u2514\u2500 background_operations_assignee.trigger()  \u2014 wake up merger\n```\n\n### Key Details\n\n1. **Block splitting** (`MergeTreeDataWriter::splitBlockIntoParts`): The incoming block is hashed on partition key columns and scattered into per-partition sub-blocks.\n\n2. **Sorting** (`writeTempPartImpl`): Rows are sorted in-memory by the primary/sorting key using a stable permutation. If `optimize_row_order=true`, an additional row-order optimisation is applied.\n\n3. **Merging on insert**: For specialised engines (ReplacingMergeTree, SummingMergeTree, etc.), `mergeBlock()` runs the appropriate `IMergingAlgorithm` on the single sorted block before writing.\n\n4. **Part naming**: `MergeTreePartInfo::getPartNameV1()` produces the final name `{partition}_{min}_{max}_{level}`. While writing, the directory is prefixed with `tmp_insert_`.\n\n5. **Transaction commit**: `MergeTreeData::Transaction::commit()` atomically moves the part from `PreActive` to `Active` in the in-memory set, making it visible to `SELECT` queries.\n\n**Key source files**:\n- `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeSink.cpp` \u2014 consume/finalize pipeline\n- `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeDataWriter.cpp` \u2014 core write logic\n- `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergedBlockOutputStream.cpp` \u2014 streaming column writer\n- `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeDataPartWriterWide.cpp` \u2014 Wide format column writer\n- `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeDataPartWriterCompact.cpp` \u2014 Compact format writer\n\n---\n\n## 4. Merge Path: Background Merges\n\n### Overview\n\nBackground merges are triggered by `BackgroundJobsAssignee` immediately after a successful INSERT. The merge process reduces part count, reclaims space (via TTL / deduplication), and keeps query performance high.\n\n### Flow Diagram\n\n```\nBackgroundJobsAssignee::trigger()         [BackgroundJobsAssignee.cpp]\n      \u2502\n      \u25bc\nMergePlainMergeTreeTask::executeStep()    [MergePlainMergeTreeTask.cpp]\n      \u2502\n      \u25bc\nMergeTreeDataMergerMutator::selectPartsToMerge()\n      \u2502                              [MergeTreeDataMergerMutator.cpp]\n      \u251c\u2500 Step 1: getDataPartsToSelectMergeFrom()\n      \u2502     \u2014 collect all Active parts (respecting transactions)\n      \u2502\n      \u251c\u2500 Step 2: getPossibleMergeRanges()\n      \u2502     \u2014 split parts into contiguous mergeable ranges using\n      \u2502       can_merge_callback (no gaps allowed between blocks)\n      \u2502\n      \u2514\u2500 Step 3: selectPartsToMergeFromRanges()\n            \u2014 apply SimpleMergeSelector / TTLMergeSelector heuristics\n              (balance part sizes, prefer newer partitions, respect\n               max_bytes_to_merge_at_max_space_in_pool setting)\n      \u2502\n      \u25bc\nMergeTask (coroutine)                     [MergeTask.cpp / MergeTask.h]\n      \u2502\n      \u251c\u2500 Stage 1: ExecuteAndFinalizeHorizontalPart\n      \u2502     \u251c\u2500 Open MergeTreeSequentialSource on each source part\n      \u2502     \u251c\u2500 Feed streams into MergingSortedTransform (k-way merge sort)\n      \u2502     \u2502   (or ReplacingSorted / CollapsingSorted / SummingSorted etc.)\n      \u2502     \u251c\u2500 Write merged blocks via MergedBlockOutputStream\n      \u2502     \u2502     \u2192 new <col>.bin, <col>.mrk2, primary.idx\n      \u2502     \u2514\u2500 Suspends between blocks (coroutine yield)\n      \u2502\n      \u251c\u2500 Stage 2: MergeVerticalStage (for Wide parts with many columns)\n      \u2502     \u2014 re-reads remaining columns and writes them independently,\n      \u2502       using ColumnGathererTransform guided by the row sources\n      \u2502       file produced in Stage 1\n      \u2502\n      \u2514\u2500 Stage 3: MergeProjectionStage\n            \u2014 re-materialise each projection defined on the table\n      \u2502\n      \u25bc\nMergeTreeData::Transaction::commit()\n      \u2014 new merged part becomes Active\n      \u2014 source parts become Outdated \u2192 eventually Deleting \u2192 removed\n```\n\n### Merge Selection Heuristics\n\n`SimpleMergeSelector` (the default) uses a score-based algorithm:\n- Prefers merging parts of similar sizes (exponential base factor).\n- Respects `max_bytes_to_merge_at_max_space_in_pool` / `max_bytes_to_merge_at_min_space_in_pool` thresholds (interpolated based on pool saturation).\n- `TTLMergeSelector` is invoked instead when TTL-expired parts need compaction.\n\n**Key source files**:\n- `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeDataMergerMutator.cpp` \u2014 part selection logic\n- `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTask.cpp` \u2014 merge coroutine implementation\n- `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeSelectors/SimpleMergeSelector.cpp` \u2014 scoring algorithm\n- `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeSelectors/TTLMergeSelector.cpp` \u2014 TTL-aware selector\n- `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergedBlockOutputStream.cpp` \u2014 merged output writer\n- `src/Storages/MergeTree/FutureMergedMutatedPart.h` \u2014 represents the planned new part\n\n---\n\n## 5. Read Path: SELECT with Index Skipping\n\n### Flow Diagram\n\n```\nSELECT query\n      \u2502\n      \u25bc\nMergeTreeDataSelectExecutor::read()\n      \u2502                          [MergeTreeDataSelectExecutor.cpp]\n      \u251c\u2500 Acquire snapshot: list of Active DataParts at query start\n      \u2502\n      \u251c\u2500 Partition pruning (PartitionPruner)\n      \u2502     \u2014 evaluate partition key condition against part's\n      \u2502       minmax_<col>.idx \u2192 skip entire partitions\n      \u2502     [PartitionPruner.cpp]\n      \u2502\n      \u251c\u2500 Per-part primary key scan (markRangesFromPKRange)\n      \u2502     \u2014 binary search on primary.idx loaded into memory\n      \u2502     \u2014 produces MarkRanges: list of [begin_mark, end_mark) intervals\n      \u2502     \u2014 coarse (8\u00d7index_granularity) then fine granularity scan\n      \u2502\n      \u251c\u2500 Skip index filtering (filterMarksUsingIndex)\n      \u2502     \u2014 for each secondary index (bloom filter, minmax, set, etc.)\n      \u2502       read the .idx file and eliminate mark ranges that cannot\n      \u2502       contain matching rows\n      \u2502     [MergeTreeIndexReader.cpp, MergeTreeIndices.h]\n      \u2502\n      \u251c\u2500 Build ReadFromMergeTree query plan step\n      \u2502     \u2014 distributes RangesInDataPart across N threads via\n      \u2502       MergeTreeReadPool / MergeTreePrefetchedReadPool\n      \u2502     [ReadFromMergeTree.cpp, MergeTreeReadPool.cpp]\n      \u2502\n      \u2514\u2500 Per-thread MergeTreeSelectProcessor\n            \u2502                      [MergeTreeSelectProcessor.cpp]\n            \u2514\u2500 MergeTreeRangeReader\n                  \u2014 reads granule-by-granule from .bin via\n                    CompressedReadBufferFromFile\n                  \u2014 applies PREWHERE filtering before reading\n                    remaining columns (columnar short-circuit)\n                  [MergeTreeRangeReader.cpp]\n```\n\n### Key Optimizations\n\n1. **Partition pruning**: Entire partitions skipped without touching any data files, based on `minmax_<col>.idx`.\n\n2. **Primary key binary search**: The sparse primary index (`primary.idx`) is loaded into memory (or served from `PrimaryIndexCache`). A binary search over this index identifies candidate mark ranges. Only the matching granules (8192 rows each by default) are read.\n\n3. **Skip indices**: After primary-key pruning, secondary skip indices further eliminate mark ranges:\n   - **MinMax** \u2014 range condition on a column\n   - **Set** \u2014 IN-condition with a known small set\n   - **Bloom filter** \u2014 probabilistic membership test\n   - **Full-text / Gin** \u2014 inverted index for text search\n   - **Vector similarity** \u2014 ANN index for approximate nearest neighbour\n\n4. **PREWHERE optimisation** (`MergeTreeWhereOptimizer`): Heavy filter predicates are moved to PREWHERE and evaluated first on the cheapest columns, avoiding reads of other columns for non-matching rows.\n\n5. **Mark cache** (`MarkCache`): `.mrk2` files are cached in-process to avoid repeated disk seeks.\n\n6. **Parallel reading**: `MergeTreeReadPool` distributes mark ranges across multiple threads; `MergeTreePrefetchedReadPool` adds async prefetch for remote storage.\n\n**Key source files**:\n- `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeDataSelectExecutor.cpp` \u2014 top-level read orchestration\n- `src/Storages/MergeTree/KeyCondition.cpp` \u2014 primary key condition & binary search\n- `src/Storages/MergeTree/PartitionPruner.cpp` \u2014 partition elimination\n- `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeRangeReader.cpp` \u2014 column-at-a-time granule reader\n- `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeReadPool.cpp` \u2014 thread work distribution\n- `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeIndexReader.cpp` \u2014 secondary index evaluation\n- `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeWhereOptimizer.cpp` \u2014 PREWHERE optimisation\n\n---\n\n## 6. Key Source Files Summary\n\n| File | Role |\n|------|------|\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeData.h` | Base class for all MergeTree variants; owns the data-parts registry (`data_parts`), `MergingParams`, `Transaction` commit/rollback |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeData.cpp` | Part lifecycle management: add, remove, rename, prune; background task scheduling |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/IMergeTreeDataPart.h` | Abstract base for a data part; stores rows_count, index_granularity, MinMaxIndex, checksums, TTL info, part state |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreePartInfo.h` | `MergeTreePartInfo` struct: partition_id, min/max block, level, mutation; part containment logic |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeDataWriter.cpp` | `writeTempPart()`: sort, merge-on-insert, write columns/marks/primary index for a single block |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeSink.cpp` | Pipeline sink: receives chunks, calls writer, commits transaction, triggers merge |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeDataMergerMutator.cpp` | Three-step merge selection: collect parts \u2192 build ranges \u2192 apply selector heuristic |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTask.cpp` / `MergeTask.h` | Coroutine-based merge execution in three stages: horizontal, vertical, projections |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeDataSelectExecutor.cpp` | `read()` entry point: partition pruning, primary key scan, skip-index filtering, query plan construction |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/KeyCondition.cpp` | Converts WHERE/PREWHERE to a key condition; `markRangesFromPKRange()` binary-searches the primary index |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeRangeReader.cpp` | Reads mark ranges from `.bin` files column by column; implements PREWHERE short-circuit |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeIndexGranularityInfo.h` | Fixed vs. adaptive granularity configuration; mark file extension selection |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeDataPartWriterWide.cpp` | Writes one `.bin`/`.mrk2` pair per column in Wide format; computes marks per granule |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergedBlockOutputStream.cpp` | High-level merge output stream used by both merges and mutations |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeDataPartState.h` | State machine enum: Temporary \u2192 PreActive \u2192 Active \u2192 Outdated \u2192 Deleting |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/PartitionPruner.cpp` | Evaluates partition condition against part min/max; eliminates whole parts before any I/O |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeReadPool.cpp` | Distributes mark ranges across reader threads; supports in-order and parallel-replicas modes |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeSelectors/SimpleMergeSelector.cpp` | Core merge heuristic: scores part ranges by size balance and age |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/BackgroundJobsAssignee.cpp` | Schedules merges/mutations/moves on the background thread pool |\n\n---\n\n## 7. MergeTree Engine Variants\n\nThe `MergeTreeData::MergingParams::Mode` enum selects additional processing applied during both insert-time `mergeBlock()` and background merges:\n\n| Mode | Engine | Merge Behaviour |\n|------|--------|----------------|\n| `Ordinary` (0) | MergeTree | No deduplication; rows are preserved as-is |\n| `Collapsing` (1) | CollapsingMergeTree | Cancel pairs of rows with opposite `sign` column values |\n| `Summing` (2) | SummingMergeTree | Sum numeric columns for identical primary key rows |\n| `Aggregating` (3) | AggregatingMergeTree | Merge aggregate function states |\n| `Replacing` (5) | ReplacingMergeTree | Keep only the latest version of each primary key |\n| `Graphite` (6) | GraphiteMergeTree | Time-series rollup for Graphite metrics |\n| `VersionedCollapsing` (7) | VersionedCollapsingMergeTree | Version-aware collapse with sign column |\n\n**Source**: `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeData.h` (lines 339\u2013351)\n\n---\n\n## 8. Replication Layer\n\nFor `ReplicatedMergeTree`, all merges and mutations are coordinated via ZooKeeper:\n- Each replica maintains a `/replicas/<name>/queue` of log entries.\n- `ReplicatedMergeTreeQueue` (`src/Storages/MergeTree/ReplicatedMergeTreeQueue.cpp`) applies entries (merges, mutations, fetches) in order.\n- `MergeFromLogEntryTask` and `MutateFromLogEntryTask` wrap `MergeTask` / `MutateTask`.\n- Part replication between replicas uses `DataPartsExchange` (`src/Storages/MergeTree/DataPartsExchange.cpp`).\n",

\u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510 \u2502\n\u2502  \u2502MergeTree \u2502   \u2502MergeTreeData     \u2502   \u2502MergeTreeDataMerger  \u2502 \u2502\n\u2502  \u2502   Sink   \u2502   \u2502SelectExecutor    \u2502   \u2502    Mutator          \u2502 \u2502\n\u2502  \u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u252c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518   \u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u252c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518   \u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u252c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518 \u2502\n\u2502       \u2502                  \u2502                         \u2502            \u2502\n\u2502       \u25bc                  \u2502                         \u25bc            \u2502\n\u2502  \u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510            \u2502             \u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510 \u2502\n\u2502  \u2502MergeTree \u2502            \u2502             \u2502     MergeTask       \u2502 \u2502\n\u2502  \u2502DataWriter\u2502            \u2502             \u2502  (coroutine-based)  \u2502 \u2502\n\u2502  \u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u252c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518            \u2502               \u2502            \u2502\n\u2502       \u25bc                  \u25bc                         \u25bc            \u2502\n\u2502  \u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510   \u2502\n\u2502  \u2502                  MergeTreeData                          \u2502   \u2502\n\u2502  \u2502            (Central data part registry)                 \u2502   \u2502\n\u2502  \u2502  data_parts: boost::multi_index_container<DataPartPtr>  \u2502   \u2502\n\u2502  \u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u252c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518   \u2502\n\u2502                             \u2502                                   \u2502\n\u2502                             \u25bc                                   \u2502\n\u2502  \u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510  \u2502\n\u2502  \u2502               Data Parts on Disk                         \u2502  \u2502\n\u2502  \u2502  partition_id_minBlock_maxBlock_level/                   \u2502  \u2502\n\u2502  \u2502    columns.txt   checksums.txt   primary.idx             \u2502  \u2502\n\u2502  \u2502    [col].bin     [col].mrk2      [idx].idx               \u2502  \u2502\n\u2502  \u2502\n\u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518\n```\n\n## 2. Data Part Structure\n\nA data part is the fundamental unit of storage in MergeTree. Each INSERT creates one or more parts; background merges combine multiple parts into one.\n\n### Part Directory Naming Convention\n\n```\n{partition_id}_{min_block}_{max_block}_{level}[_{mutation}]/\n```\n\n- **partition_id**: hash or value of the partition expression\n- **min_block / max_block**: monotonically-increasing block numbers covering the inserted range\n- **level**: merge depth (0 = freshly inserted, increments with each merge)\n- **mutation**: mutation version (appended after mutations)\n\nExamples: `all_1_1_0`, `all_1_3_1`, `20240101_5_10_2_42`\n\n**Source**: `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreePartInfo.h` \u2014 `struct MergeTreePartInfo`\n\n### Files Inside a Data Part (Wide Format)\n\n```\n<part_dir>/\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 columns.txt          \u2014 list of columns and their data types\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 checksums.txt        \u2014 file sizes and SHA256 checksums for data integrity\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 count.txt            \u2014 total number of rows\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 primary.idx          \u2014 sparse primary key index (one entry per granule)\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 partition.dat        \u2014 serialized partition key value\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 minmax_<col>.idx     \u2014 min/max index per column in the partition key\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 <column>.bin         \u2014 compressed column data (LZ4 / ZSTD)\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 <column>.mrk2        \u2014 mark file: (compressed_offset, uncompressed_offset) per granule\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 skp_idx_<name>.idx   \u2014 data-skipping (secondary) index data\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 skp_idx_<name>.mrk2  \u2014 mark file for the skip index\n\u2514\u2500\u2500 metadata_version.txt \u2014 schema metadata version\n```\n\nFor **Compact** format (small parts), all columns are stored in a single `data.bin` / `data.mrk2` file pair.\n\n**Source**: `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeData.h` (lines 120\u2013135 comments), `src/Storages/MergeTree/IMergeTreeDataPart.h`\n\n### Part Format Types\n\n| Type    | Layout                                  | When used                     |\n|---------|-----------------------------------------|-------------------------------|\n| Wide    | One `.bin` + `.mrk2` per column         | Large parts (many rows/bytes) |\n| Compact | Single `data.bin` + `data.mrk2`         | Small parts (fresh inserts)   |\n\n**Source**: `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeDataPartWide.h`, `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeDataPartCompact.h`\n\n### Index Granularity\n\nThe primary index is **sparse** \u2014 one index entry is stored for every `index_granularity` rows (default: 8192). Each granule corresponds to a mark in the `.mrk2` file, which records byte offsets into the `.bin` file for efficient random seeks.\n\n**Source**: `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeIndexGranularity.h`, `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeIndexGranularityInfo.h`\n\n### Part Lifecycle (State Machine)\n\n```\nTemporary \u2192 PreActive \u2192 Active \u2192 Outdated \u2192 Deleting \u2192 (deleted)\n                \u2193\n            Outdated  (rollback on failure)\n```\n\n**Source**: `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeDataPartState.h`\n\n---\n\n## 3. Write Path: INSERT to Committed Part\n\n### Flow Diagram\n\n```\nINSERT statement\n      \u2502\n      \u25bc\nMergeTreeSink::consume()          [src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeSink.cpp]\n      \u2502\n      \u251c\u2500 splitBlockIntoParts()    \u2014 split block by partition key into sub-blocks\n      \u2502     [MergeTreeDataWriter.cpp]\n      \u2502\n      \u251c\u2500 writeTempPart()          \u2014 create a temporary part per partition\n      \u2502     [MergeTreeDataWriter.cpp]\n      \u2502     \u2502\n      \u2502     \u251c\u2500 Evaluate partition key expression\n      \u2502     \u251c\u2500 Build MinMaxIndex (per-part min/max for partitioning columns)\n      \u2502     \u251c\u2500 Evaluate sorting key expression\n      \u2502     \u251c\u2500 Sort rows by primary key (stableGetPermutation)\n      \u2502     \u251c\u2500 Optionally apply merging algorithm (Replacing, Summing, etc.)\n      \u2502     \u251c\u2500 Write column data    \u2192 <col>.bin\n      \u2502     \u251c\u2500 Write mark file      \u2192 <col>.mrk2\n      \u2502     \u251c\u2500 Write primary.idx    (one entry per granule)\n      \u2502     \u2514\u2500 Write skip index files (if materialize_skip_indexes_on_insert=1)\n      \u2502\n      \u2514\u2500 finishDelayedChunk()\n            \u2502\n            \u251c\u2500 temp_part.finalize()         \u2014 flush buffers + optional fsync\n            \u251c\u2500 lockParts()\n            \u251c\u2500 renameTempPartAndAdd()       \u2014 rename tmp_insert_XXX \u2192 final name\n            \u251c\u2500 transaction.commit()         \u2014 part state: PreActive \u2192 Active\n            \u2514\u2500 background_operations_assignee.trigger()  \u2014 wake up merger\n```\n\n### Key Details\n\n1. **Block splitting** (`MergeTreeDataWriter::splitBlockIntoParts`): The incoming block is hashed on partition key columns using `buildScatterSelector()` and scattered into per-partition sub-blocks.\n\n2. **Sorting** (`writeTempPartImpl`): Rows are sorted in-memory by the primary/sorting key using a stable permutation. If `optimize_row_order=true`, an additional row-order optimization (Hilbert curve locality) is applied.\n\n3. **Merging on insert**: For specialised engines (ReplacingMergeTree, SummingMergeTree, etc.), `mergeBlock()` runs the appropriate `IMergingAlgorithm` on the single sorted block before writing, pre-collapsing redundant rows.\n\n4. **Part naming**: `MergeTreePartInfo::getPartNameV1()` produces the final name `{partition}_{min}_{max}_{level}`. While writing, the directory is prefixed with `tmp_insert_`.\n\n5. **Transaction commit**: `MergeTreeData::Transaction::commit()` atomically moves the part from `PreActive` to `Active` in the in-memory `data_parts` set, making it immediately visible to `SELECT` queries.\n\n**Key source files**:\n- `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeSink.cpp` \u2014 consume/finalize pipeline\n- `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeDataWriter.cpp` \u2014 core write logic (sorting, block splitting, temp part creation)\n- `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergedBlockOutputStream.cpp` \u2014 streaming column writer used during write\n- `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeDataPartWriterWide.cpp` \u2014 Wide format column writer (per-column streams)\n- `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeDataPartWriterCompact.cpp` \u2014 Compact format writer (single stream)\n\n---\n\n## 4. Merge Path: Background Merges\n\n### Overview\n\nBackground merges are triggered by `BackgroundJobsAssignee` after successful INSERTs. The merge process reduces part count, reclaims space via TTL / deduplication, and keeps read performance high by consolidating small parts.\n\n### Flow Diagram\n\n```\nBackgroundJobsAssignee::trigger()         [BackgroundJobsAssignee.cpp]\n      \u2502\n      \u25bc\nMergePlainMergeTreeTask::executeStep()    [MergePlainMergeTreeTask.cpp]\n      \u2502\n      \u25bc\nMergeTreeDataMergerMutator::selectPartsToMerge()\n      \u2502                              [MergeTreeDataMergerMutator.cpp]\n      \u251c\u2500 Step 1: getDataPartsToSelectMergeFrom()\n      \u2502     \u2014 collect all Active parts (respecting transactions)\n      \u2502\n      \u251c\u2500 Step 2: getPossibleMergeRanges()\n      \u2502     \u2014 split parts into contiguous mergeable ranges using\n      \u2502       can_merge_callback (no inter-part gaps allowed within range)\n      \u2502\n      \u2514\u2500 Step 3: selectPartsToMergeFromRanges()\n            \u2014 apply SimpleMergeSelector / TTLMergeSelector heuristics\n              (balance part sizes, respect max_bytes_to_merge_at_max_space_in_pool)\n      \u2502\n      \u25bc\nMergeTask (coroutine)                     [MergeTask.cpp / MergeTask.h]\n      \u2502\n      \u251c\u2500 Stage 1: ExecuteAndFinalizeHorizontalPart\n      \u2502     \u251c\u2500 Open MergeTreeSequentialSource on each source part\n      \u2502     \u251c\u2500 Feed streams into MergingSortedTransform (k-way merge sort)\n      \u2502     \u2502   (or ReplacingSorted / CollapsingSorted / SummingSorted etc.)\n      \u2502     \u251c\u2500 Write merged blocks via MergedBlockOutputStream\n      \u2502     \u2502     \u2192 new <col>.bin, <col>.mrk2, primary.idx\n      \u2502     \u2514\u2500 Suspends between blocks (coroutine yield for cooperative scheduling)\n      \u2502\n      \u251c\u2500 Stage 2: MergeVerticalStage (for Wide parts with many columns)\n      \u2502     \u2014 re-reads remaining columns independently using ColumnGathererTransform\n      \u2502       guided by the row-sources file produced in Stage 1\n      \u2502\n      \u2514\u2500 Stage 3: MergeProjectionStage\n            \u2014 re-materialise each projection defined on the table\n      \u2502\n      \u25bc\nMergeTreeData::Transaction::commit()\n      \u2014 new merged part becomes Active\n      \u2014 source parts become Outdated \u2192 eventually Deleting \u2192 removed from disk\n```\n\n### Merge Selection Heuristics\n\n`SimpleMergeSelector` (the default) uses a score-based algorithm:\n- Prefers merging parts of similar sizes (configurable exponential base factor via `merge_selector_base`).\n- Respects `max_bytes_to_merge_at_max_space_in_pool` / `max_bytes_to_merge_at_min_space_in_pool` thresholds, interpolated based on background pool saturation.\n- `TTLMergeSelector` is invoked instead when TTL-expired parts need compaction.\n- Pool entries are tracked via `CurrentMetrics::BackgroundMergesAndMutationsPoolTask`.\n\n**Key source files**:\n- `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeDataMergerMutator.cpp` \u2014 three-step part selection logic\n- `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTask.cpp` / `MergeTask.h` \u2014 merge coroutine (three stages)\n- `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeSelectors/SimpleMergeSelector.cpp` \u2014 scoring algorithm\n- `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeSelectors/TTLMergeSelector.cpp` \u2014 TTL-aware selector\n- `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergedBlockOutputStream.cpp` \u2014 merged output writer\n- `src/Storages/MergeTree/FutureMergedMutatedPart.h` \u2014 descriptor of the planned new part\n\n---\n\n## 5. Read Path: SELECT with Index Skipping\n\n### Flow Diagram\n\n```\nSELECT query\n      \u2502\n      \u25bc\nMergeTreeDataSelectExecutor::read()\n      \u2502                          [MergeTreeDataSelectExecutor.cpp]\n      \u251c\u2500 Acquire snapshot of Active DataParts at query start\n      \u2502\n      \u251c\u2500 Partition pruning (PartitionPruner)\n      \u2502     \u2014 evaluate partition key condition against each part's\n      \u2502       minmax_<col>.idx \u2192 skip entire partitions without I/O\n      \u2502     [src/Storages/MergeTree/PartitionPruner.cpp]\n      \u2502\n      \u251c\u2500 Per-part primary key scan (markRangesFromPKRange)\n      \u2502     \u2014 load primary.idx into memory (or serve from PrimaryIndexCache)\n      \u2502     \u2014 binary search produces MarkRanges: [begin_mark, end_mark) intervals\n      \u2502     \u2014 coarse pass (merge_tree_coarse_index_granularity \u00d7 granule_size)\n      \u2502       then fine pass at granule resolution\n      \u2502     [src/Storages/MergeTree/KeyCondition.cpp]\n      \u2502\n      \u251c\u2500 Skip index filtering (filterMarksUsingIndex)\n      \u2502     \u2014 for each secondary index (bloom filter, minmax, set, etc.)\n      \u2502       read the .idx file, evaluate condition, eliminate non-matching\n      \u2502       mark ranges before any column data is read\n      \u2502     [src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeIndexReader.cpp]\n      \u2502\n      \u251c\u2500 Build ReadFromMergeTree query plan step\n      \u2502     \u2014 distributes RangesInDataPart across N reader threads via\n      \u2502       MergeTreeReadPool / MergeTreePrefetchedReadPool\n      \u2502     [src/Processors/QueryPlan/ReadFromMergeTree.cpp]\n      \u2502     [src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeReadPool.cpp]\n      \u2502\n      \u2514\u2500 Per-thread MergeTreeSelectProcessor\n            \u2502                      [src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeSelectProcessor.cpp]\n            \u2514\u2500 MergeTreeRangeReader\n                  \u2014 reads granule-by-granule from .bin via\n                    CompressedReadBufferFromFile, seeking to marks in .mrk2\n                  \u2014 applies PREWHERE filtering before reading remaining columns\n                    (columnar short-circuit: unread columns save I/O)\n                  [src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeRangeReader.cpp]\n```\n\n### Key Optimizations\n\n1. **Partition pruning**: Entire partitions are skipped without touching any column data files, based on `minmax_<col>.idx` stored per part.\n\n2. **Primary key binary search**: The sparse primary index (`primary.idx`) is loaded into memory (or served from `PrimaryIndexCache`). Binary search over this index identifies candidate mark ranges. Only the matching granules (8192 rows each by default) are read from disk.\n\n3. **Skip indices**: After primary-key pruning, secondary skip indices further eliminate mark ranges before any column data is read:\n   - **MinMax** \u2014 range condition on a column (`src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeIndexMinMax.cpp`)\n   - **Set** \u2014 IN-condition with a known small set (`src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeIndexSet.cpp`)\n   - **Bloom filter** \u2014 probabilistic membership test (`src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeIndexBloomFilter.cpp`)\n   - **Full-text / Gin** \u2014 inverted index for text search (`src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeIndexFullText.cpp`)\n   - **Vector similarity** \u2014 ANN index for approximate nearest-neighbour (`src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeIndexVectorSimilarity.cpp`)\n\n4. **PREWHERE optimisation** (`MergeTreeWhereOptimizer`): Heavy filter predicates are moved to PREWHERE and evaluated first on the cheapest/smallest columns, avoiding reads of other columns for non-matching rows.\n\n5. **Mark cache** (`MarkCache`): `.mrk2` files are cached in-process to avoid repeated disk seeks on repeated queries.\n\n6. **Parallel reading**: `MergeTreeReadPool` distributes mark ranges across multiple threads; `MergeTreePrefetchedReadPool` (`src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreePrefetchedReadPool.cpp`) adds async prefetch for remote (S3/HDFS) storage.\n\n**Key source files**:\n- `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeDataSelectExecutor.cpp` \u2014 top-level read orchestration\n- `src/Storages/MergeTree/KeyCondition.cpp` \u2014 primary key condition & binary search (`markRangesFromPKRange`)\n- `src/Storages/MergeTree/PartitionPruner.cpp` \u2014 partition elimination\n- `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeRangeReader.cpp` \u2014 column-at-a-time granule reader with PREWHERE\n- `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeReadPool.cpp` \u2014 thread work distribution\n- `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeIndexReader.cpp` \u2014 secondary index evaluation\n- `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeWhereOptimizer.cpp` \u2014 PREWHERE optimisation\n\n---\n\n## 6. Key Source Files Summary\n\n| File | Role |\n|------|------|\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeData.h` | Base class for all MergeTree variants; owns the `data_parts` registry, `MergingParams`, `Transaction` commit/rollback |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeData.cpp` | Part lifecycle management: add, remove, rename, prune; background task scheduling |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/IMergeTreeDataPart.h` | Abstract base for a data part; stores rows_count, index_granularity, MinMaxIndex, checksums, TTL info, part state |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreePartInfo.h` | `MergeTreePartInfo` struct: partition_id, min/max block, level, mutation; part containment / disjointness logic |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeDataPartState.h` | State machine enum: Temporary \u2192 PreActive \u2192 Active \u2192 Outdated \u2192 Deleting |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeDataWriter.cpp` | `writeTempPart()`: sort, merge-on-insert, write columns/marks/primary index for a single block |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeSink.cpp` | Pipeline sink: receives chunks, calls writer, commits transaction, triggers merge |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeDataPartWriterWide.cpp` | Writes one `.bin`/`.mrk2` pair per column in Wide format; computes marks per granule |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeDataPartWriterCompact.cpp` | Writes all columns into a single `data.bin`/`data.mrk2` for Compact format |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergedBlockOutputStream.cpp` | High-level merge output stream used by both merges and mutations |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeDataMergerMutator.cpp` | Three-step merge selection: collect parts \u2192 build ranges \u2192 apply selector heuristic |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTask.cpp` | Coroutine-based merge execution in three stages: horizontal, vertical, projections |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTask.h` | MergeTask interface, stage definitions, GlobalRuntimeContext |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeDataSelectExecutor.cpp` | `read()` entry point: partition pruning, primary key scan, skip-index filtering, query plan construction |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/KeyCondition.cpp` | Converts WHERE/PREWHERE to a key condition; `markRangesFromPKRange()` binary-searches the primary index |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/PartitionPruner.cpp` | Evaluates partition condition against part min/max; eliminates whole parts before any I/O |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeRangeReader.cpp` | Reads mark ranges from `.bin` files column by column; implements PREWHERE short-circuit |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeReadPool.cpp` | Distributes mark ranges across reader threads; supports in-order and parallel-replicas modes |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreePrefetchedReadPool.cpp` | Async prefetch read pool for remote storage (S3, HDFS) |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeIndexReader.cpp` | Reads and evaluates secondary (skip) index files to eliminate mark ranges |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeWhereOptimizer.cpp` | Moves expensive filter conditions to PREWHERE to reduce column reads |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeIndexGranularityInfo.h` | Fixed vs. adaptive granularity configuration; mark file extension selection |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/BackgroundJobsAssignee.cpp` | Schedules merges/mutations/moves onto the background thread pool |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeSelectors/SimpleMergeSelector.cpp` | Core merge heuristic: scores part ranges by size balance and part age |\n\n---\n\n## 7. MergeTree Engine Variants\n\nThe `MergeTreeData::MergingParams::Mode` enum selects additional processing applied during both insert-time `mergeBlock()` and background merges:\n\n| Mode | Engine | Merge Behaviour |\n|------|--------|----------------|\n| `Ordinary` (0) | MergeTree | No deduplication; all rows preserved |\n| `Collapsing` (1) | CollapsingMergeTree | Cancel pairs of rows with opposite `sign` column values |\n| `Summing` (2) | SummingMergeTree | Sum numeric columns for identical primary key rows |\n| `Aggregating` (3) | AggregatingMergeTree | Merge aggregate function states |\n| `Replacing` (5) | ReplacingMergeTree | Keep only the latest version of each primary key |\n| `Graphite` (6) | GraphiteMergeTree | Time-series rollup for Graphite metrics |\n| `VersionedCollapsing` (7) | VersionedCollapsingMergeTree | Version-aware collapse with sign column |\n\n**Source**: `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeData.h` (lines 339\u2013351)\n\n---\n\n## 8. Replication Layer\n\nFor `ReplicatedMergeTree`, all merges and mutations are coordinated via ZooKeeper:\n- Each replica maintains a `/replicas/<name>/queue` of log entries.\n- `ReplicatedMergeTreeQueue` (`src/Storages/MergeTree/ReplicatedMergeTreeQueue.cpp`) applies entries (merges, mutations, fetches) in order.\n- `MergeFromLogEntryTask` (`src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeFromLogEntryTask.cpp`) and `MutateFromLogEntryTask` wrap `MergeTask` / `MutateTask`.\n- Part replication between replicas uses `DataPartsExchange` (`src/Storages/MergeTree/DataPartsExchange.cpp`).\n",

2. Data Part Structure\n\nA data part is the fundamental unit of storage in MergeTree. Each INSERT creates one or more parts; background merges combine multiple parts into one.\n\n### Part Directory Naming Convention\n\n```\n{partition_id}_{min_block}_{max_block}_{level}[_{mutation}]/\n```\n\n- **partition_id**: hash or value of the partition expression\n- **min_block / max_block**: monotonically-increasing block numbers covering the inserted range\n- **level**: merge depth (0 = freshly inserted, increments with each merge)\n- **mutation**: mutation version (appended after mutations)\n\nExamples: `all_1_1_0`, `all_1_3_1`, `20240101_5_10_2_42`\n\n**Source**: `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreePartInfo.h` \u2014 `struct MergeTreePartInfo`\n\n### Files Inside a Data Part (Wide Format)\n\n```\n<part_dir>/\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 columns.txt          \u2014 list of columns and their data types\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 checksums.txt        \u2014 file sizes and SHA256 checksums for data integrity\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 count.txt            \u2014 total number of rows\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 primary.idx          \u2014 sparse primary key index (one entry per granule)\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 partition.dat        \u2014 serialized partition key value\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 minmax_<col>.idx     \u2014 min/max index per column in the partition key\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 <column>.bin         \u2014 compressed column data (LZ4 / ZSTD)\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 <column>.mrk2        \u2014 mark file: (compressed_offset, uncompressed_offset) per granule\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 skp_idx_<name>.idx   \u2014 data-skipping (secondary) index data\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 skp_idx_<name>.mrk2  \u2014 mark file for the skip index\n\u2514\u2500\u2500 metadata_version.txt \u2014 schema metadata version\n```\n\nFor **Compact** format (small parts), all columns are stored in a single `data.bin` / `data.mrk2` file pair.\n\n**Source**: `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeData.h` (lines 120\u2013135 comments), `src/Storages/MergeTree/IMergeTreeDataPart.h`\n\n### Part Format Types\n\n| Type    | Layout                                  | When used                     |\n|---------|-----------------------------------------|-------------------------------|\n| Wide    | One `.bin` + `.mrk2` per column         | Large parts (many rows/bytes) |\n| Compact | Single `data.bin` + `data.mrk2`         | Small parts (fresh inserts)   |\n\n**Source**: `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeDataPartWide.h`, `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeDataPartCompact.h`\n\n### Index Granularity\n\nThe primary index is **sparse** \u2014 one index entry is stored for every `index_granularity` rows (default: 8192). Each granule corresponds to a mark in the `.mrk2` file, which records byte offsets into the `.bin` file for efficient random seeks.\n\n**Source**: `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeIndexGranularity.h`, `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeIndexGranularityInfo.h`\n\n### Part Lifecycle (State Machine)\n\n```\nTemporary \u2192 PreActive \u2192 Active \u2192 Outdated \u2192 Deleting \u2192 (deleted)\n                \u2193\n            Outdated  (rollback on failure)\n```\n\n**Source**: `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeDataPartState.h`\n\n---\n\n## 3. Write Path: INSERT to Committed Part\n\n### Flow Diagram\n\n```\nINSERT statement\n      \u2502\n      \u25bc\nMergeTreeSink::consume()          [src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeSink.cpp]\n      \u2502\n      \u251c\u2500 splitBlockIntoParts()    \u2014 split block by partition key into sub-blocks\n      \u2502     [MergeTreeDataWriter.cpp]\n      \u2502\n      \u251c\u2500 writeTempPart()          \u2014 create a temporary part per partition\n      \u2502     [MergeTreeDataWriter.cpp]\n      \u2502     \u2502\n      \u2502     \u251c\u2500 Evaluate partition key expression\n      \u2502     \u251c\u2500 Build MinMaxIndex (per-part min/max for partitioning columns)\n      \u2502     \u251c\u2500 Evaluate sorting key expression\n      \u2502     \u251c\u2500 Sort rows by primary key (stableGetPermutation)\n      \u2502     \u251c\u2500 Optionally apply merging algorithm (Replacing, Summing, etc.)\n      \u2502     \u251c\u2500 Write column data    \u2192 <col>.bin\n      \u2502     \u251c\u2500 Write mark file      \u2192 <col>.mrk2\n      \u2502     \u251c\u2500 Write primary.idx    (one entry per granule)\n      \u2502     \u2514\u2500 Write skip index files (if materialize_skip_indexes_on_insert=1)\n      \u2502\n      \u2514\u2500 finishDelayedChunk()\n            \u2502\n            \u251c\u2500 temp_part.finalize()         \u2014 flush buffers + optional fsync\n            \u251c\u2500 lockParts()\n            \u251c\u2500 renameTempPartAndAdd()       \u2014 rename tmp_insert_XXX \u2192 final name\n            \u251c\u2500 transaction.commit()         \u2014 part state: PreActive \u2192 Active\n            \u2514\u2500 background_operations_assignee.trigger()  \u2014 wake up merger\n```\n\n### Key Details\n\n1. **Block splitting** (`MergeTreeDataWriter::splitBlockIntoParts`): The incoming block is hashed on partition key columns using `buildScatterSelector()` and scattered into per-partition sub-blocks.\n\n2. **Sorting** (`writeTempPartImpl`): Rows are sorted in-memory by the primary/sorting key using a stable permutation. If `optimize_row_order=true`, an additional row-order optimization (Hilbert curve locality) is applied.\n\n3. **Merging on insert**: For specialised engines (ReplacingMergeTree, SummingMergeTree, etc.), `mergeBlock()` runs the appropriate `IMergingAlgorithm` on the single sorted block before writing, pre-collapsing redundant rows.\n\n4. **Part naming**: `MergeTreePartInfo::getPartNameV1()` produces the final name `{partition}_{min}_{max}_{level}`. While writing, the directory is prefixed with `tmp_insert_`.\n\n5. **Transaction commit**: `MergeTreeData::Transaction::commit()` atomically moves the part from `PreActive` to `Active` in the in-memory `data_parts` set, making it immediately visible to `SELECT` queries.\n\n**Key source files**:\n- `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeSink.cpp` \u2014 consume/finalize pipeline\n- `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeDataWriter.cpp` \u2014 core write logic (sorting, block splitting, temp part creation)\n- `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergedBlockOutputStream.cpp` \u2014 streaming column writer used during write\n- `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeDataPartWriterWide.cpp` \u2014 Wide format column writer (per-column streams)\n- `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeDataPartWriterCompact.cpp` \u2014 Compact format writer (single stream)\n\n---\n\n## 4. Merge Path: Background Merges\n\n### Overview\n\nBackground merges are triggered by `BackgroundJobsAssignee` after successful INSERTs. The merge process reduces part count, reclaims space via TTL / deduplication, and keeps read performance high by consolidating small parts.\n\n### Flow Diagram\n\n```\nBackgroundJobsAssignee::trigger()         [BackgroundJobsAssignee.cpp]\n      \u2502\n      \u25bc\nMergePlainMergeTreeTask::executeStep()    [MergePlainMergeTreeTask.cpp]\n      \u2502\n      \u25bc\nMergeTreeDataMergerMutator::selectPartsToMerge()\n      \u2502                              [MergeTreeDataMergerMutator.cpp]\n      \u251c\u2500 Step 1: getDataPartsToSelectMergeFrom()\n      \u2502     \u2014 collect all Active parts (respecting transactions)\n      \u2502\n      \u251c\u2500 Step 2: getPossibleMergeRanges()\n      \u2502     \u2014 split parts into contiguous mergeable ranges using\n      \u2502       can_merge_callback (no inter-part gaps allowed within range)\n      \u2502\n      \u2514\u2500 Step 3: selectPartsToMergeFromRanges()\n            \u2014 apply SimpleMergeSelector / TTLMergeSelector heuristics\n              (balance part sizes, respect max_bytes_to_merge_at_max_space_in_pool)\n      \u2502\n      \u25bc\nMergeTask (coroutine)                     [MergeTask.cpp / MergeTask.h]\n      \u2502\n      \u251c\u2500 Stage 1: ExecuteAndFinalizeHorizontalPart\n      \u2502     \u251c\u2500 Open MergeTreeSequentialSource on each source part\n      \u2502     \u251c\u2500 Feed streams into MergingSortedTransform (k-way merge sort)\n      \u2502     \u2502   (or ReplacingSorted / CollapsingSorted / SummingSorted etc.)\n      \u2502     \u251c\u2500 Write merged blocks via MergedBlockOutputStream\n      \u2502     \u2502     \u2192 new <col>.bin, <col>.mrk2, primary.idx\n      \u2502     \u2514\u2500 Suspends between blocks (coroutine yield for cooperative scheduling)\n      \u2502\n      \u251c\u2500 Stage 2: MergeVerticalStage (for Wide parts with many columns)\n      \u2502     \u2014 re-reads remaining columns independently using ColumnGathererTransform\n      \u2502       guided by the row-sources file produced in Stage 1\n      \u2502\n      \u2514\u2500 Stage 3: MergeProjectionStage\n            \u2014 re-materialise each projection defined on the table\n      \u2502\n      \u25bc\nMergeTreeData::Transaction::commit()\n      \u2014 new merged part becomes Active\n      \u2014 source parts become Outdated \u2192 eventually Deleting \u2192 removed from disk\n```\n\n### Merge Selection Heuristics\n\n`SimpleMergeSelector` (the default) uses a score-based algorithm:\n- Prefers merging parts of similar sizes (configurable exponential base factor via `merge_selector_base`).\n- Respects `max_bytes_to_merge_at_max_space_in_pool` / `max_bytes_to_merge_at_min_space_in_pool` thresholds, interpolated based on background pool saturation.\n- `TTLMergeSelector` is invoked instead when TTL-expired parts need compaction.\n- Pool entries are tracked via `CurrentMetrics::BackgroundMergesAndMutationsPoolTask`.\n\n**Key source files**:\n- `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeDataMergerMutator.cpp` \u2014 three-step part selection logic\n- `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTask.cpp` / `MergeTask.h` \u2014 merge coroutine (three stages)\n- `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeSelectors/SimpleMergeSelector.cpp` \u2014 scoring algorithm\n- `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeSelectors/TTLMergeSelector.cpp` \u2014 TTL-aware selector\n- `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergedBlockOutputStream.cpp` \u2014 merged output writer\n- `src/Storages/MergeTree/FutureMergedMutatedPart.h` \u2014 descriptor of the planned new part\n\n---\n\n## 5. Read Path: SELECT with Index Skipping\n\n### Flow Diagram\n\n```\nSELECT query\n      \u2502\n      \u25bc\nMergeTreeDataSelectExecutor::read()\n      \u2502                          [MergeTreeDataSelectExecutor.cpp]\n      \u251c\u2500 Acquire snapshot of Active DataParts at query start\n      \u2502\n      \u251c\u2500 Partition pruning (PartitionPruner)\n      \u2502     \u2014 evaluate partition key condition against each part's\n      \u2502       minmax_<col>.idx \u2192 skip entire partitions without I/O\n      \u2502     [src/Storages/MergeTree/PartitionPruner.cpp]\n      \u2502\n      \u251c\u2500 Per-part primary key scan (markRangesFromPKRange)\n      \u2502     \u2014 load primary.idx into memory (or serve from PrimaryIndexCache)\n      \u2502     \u2014 binary search produces MarkRanges: [begin_mark, end_mark) intervals\n      \u2502     \u2014 coarse pass (merge_tree_coarse_index_granularity \u00d7 granule_size)\n      \u2502       then fine pass at granule resolution\n      \u2502     [src/Storages/MergeTree/KeyCondition.cpp]\n      \u2502\n      \u251c\u2500 Skip index filtering (filterMarksUsingIndex)\n      \u2502     \u2014 for each secondary index (bloom filter, minmax, set, etc.)\n      \u2502       read the .idx file, evaluate condition, eliminate non-matching\n      \u2502       mark ranges before any column data is read\n      \u2502     [src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeIndexReader.cpp]\n      \u2502\n      \u251c\u2500 Build ReadFromMergeTree query plan step\n      \u2502     \u2014 distributes RangesInDataPart across N reader threads via\n      \u2502       MergeTreeReadPool / MergeTreePrefetchedReadPool\n      \u2502     [src/Processors/QueryPlan/ReadFromMergeTree.cpp]\n      \u2502     [src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeReadPool.cpp]\n      \u2502\n      \u2514\u2500 Per-thread MergeTreeSelectProcessor\n            \u2502                      [src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeSelectProcessor.cpp]\n            \u2514\u2500 MergeTreeRangeReader\n                  \u2014 reads granule-by-granule from .bin via\n                    CompressedReadBufferFromFile, seeking to marks in .mrk2\n                  \u2014 applies PREWHERE filtering before reading remaining columns\n                    (columnar short-circuit: unread columns save I/O)\n                  [src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeRangeReader.cpp]\n```\n\n### Key Optimizations\n\n1. **Partition pruning**: Entire partitions are skipped without touching any column data files, based on `minmax_<col>.idx` stored per part.\n\n2. **Primary key binary search**: The sparse primary index (`primary.idx`) is loaded into memory (or served from `PrimaryIndexCache`). Binary search over this index identifies candidate mark ranges. Only the matching granules (8192 rows each by default) are read from disk.\n\n3. **Skip indices**: After primary-key pruning, secondary skip indices further eliminate mark ranges before any column data is read:\n   - **MinMax** \u2014 range condition on a column (`src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeIndexMinMax.cpp`)\n   - **Set** \u2014 IN-condition with a known small set (`src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeIndexSet.cpp`)\n   - **Bloom filter** \u2014 probabilistic membership test (`src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeIndexBloomFilter.cpp`)\n   - **Full-text / Gin** \u2014 inverted index for text search (`src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeIndexFullText.cpp`)\n   - **Vector similarity** \u2014 ANN index for approximate nearest-neighbour (`src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeIndexVectorSimilarity.cpp`)\n\n4. **PREWHERE optimisation** (`MergeTreeWhereOptimizer`): Heavy filter predicates are moved to PREWHERE and evaluated first on the cheapest/smallest columns, avoiding reads of other columns for non-matching rows.\n\n5. **Mark cache** (`MarkCache`): `.mrk2` files are cached in-process to avoid repeated disk seeks on repeated queries.\n\n6. **Parallel reading**: `MergeTreeReadPool` distributes mark ranges across multiple threads; `MergeTreePrefetchedReadPool` (`src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreePrefetchedReadPool.cpp`) adds async prefetch for remote (S3/HDFS) storage.\n\n**Key source files**:\n- `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeDataSelectExecutor.cpp` \u2014 top-level read orchestration\n- `src/Storages/MergeTree/KeyCondition.cpp` \u2014 primary key condition & binary search (`markRangesFromPKRange`)\n- `src/Storages/MergeTree/PartitionPruner.cpp` \u2014 partition elimination\n- `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeRangeReader.cpp` \u2014 column-at-a-time granule reader with PREWHERE\n- `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeReadPool.cpp` \u2014 thread work distribution\n- `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeIndexReader.cpp` \u2014 secondary index evaluation\n- `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeWhereOptimizer.cpp` \u2014 PREWHERE optimisation\n\n---\n\n## 6. Key Source Files Summary\n\n| File | Role |\n|------|------|\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeData.h` | Base class for all MergeTree variants; owns the `data_parts` registry, `MergingParams`, `Transaction` commit/rollback |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeData.cpp` | Part lifecycle management: add, remove, rename, prune; background task scheduling |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/IMergeTreeDataPart.h` | Abstract base for a data part; stores rows_count, index_granularity, MinMaxIndex, checksums, TTL info, part state |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreePartInfo.h` | `MergeTreePartInfo` struct: partition_id, min/max block, level, mutation; part containment / disjointness logic |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeDataPartState.h` | State machine enum: Temporary \u2192 PreActive \u2192 Active \u2192 Outdated \u2192 Deleting |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeDataWriter.cpp` | `writeTempPart()`: sort, merge-on-insert, write columns/marks/primary index for a single block |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeSink.cpp` | Pipeline sink: receives chunks, calls writer, commits transaction, triggers merge |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeDataPartWriterWide.cpp` | Writes one `.bin`/`.mrk2` pair per column in Wide format; computes marks per granule |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeDataPartWriterCompact.cpp` | Writes all columns into a single `data.bin`/`data.mrk2` for Compact format |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergedBlockOutputStream.cpp` | High-level merge output stream used by both merges and mutations |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeDataMergerMutator.cpp` | Three-step merge selection: collect parts \u2192 build ranges \u2192 apply selector heuristic |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTask.cpp` | Coroutine-based merge execution in three stages: horizontal, vertical, projections |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTask.h` | MergeTask interface, stage definitions, GlobalRuntimeContext |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeDataSelectExecutor.cpp` | `read()` entry point: partition pruning, primary key scan, skip-index filtering, query plan construction |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/KeyCondition.cpp` | Converts WHERE/PREWHERE to a key condition; `markRangesFromPKRange()` binary-searches the primary index |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/PartitionPruner.cpp` | Evaluates partition condition against part min/max; eliminates whole parts before any I/O |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeRangeReader.cpp` | Reads mark ranges from `.bin` files column by column; implements PREWHERE short-circuit |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeReadPool.cpp` | Distributes mark ranges across reader threads; supports in-order and parallel-replicas modes |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreePrefetchedReadPool.cpp` | Async prefetch read pool for remote storage (S3, HDFS) |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeIndexReader.cpp` | Reads and evaluates secondary (skip) index files to eliminate mark ranges |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeWhereOptimizer.cpp` | Moves expensive filter conditions to PREWHERE to reduce column reads |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeIndexGranularityInfo.h` | Fixed vs. adaptive granularity configuration; mark file extension selection |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/BackgroundJobsAssignee.cpp` | Schedules merges/mutations/moves onto the background thread pool |\n| `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeSelectors/SimpleMergeSelector.cpp` | Core merge heuristic: scores part ranges by size balance and part age |\n\n---\n\n## 7. MergeTree Engine Variants\n\nThe `MergeTreeData::MergingParams::Mode` enum selects additional processing applied during both insert-time `mergeBlock()` and background merges:\n\n| Mode | Engine | Merge Behaviour |\n|------|--------|----------------|\n| `Ordinary` (0) | MergeTree | No deduplication; all rows preserved |\n| `Collapsing` (1) | CollapsingMergeTree | Cancel pairs of rows with opposite `sign` column values |\n| `Summing` (2) | SummingMergeTree | Sum numeric columns for identical primary key rows |\n| `Aggregating` (3) | AggregatingMergeTree | Merge aggregate function states |\n| `Replacing` (5) | ReplacingMergeTree | Keep only the latest version of each primary key |\n| `Graphite` (6) | GraphiteMergeTree | Time-series rollup for Graphite metrics |\n| `VersionedCollapsing` (7) | VersionedCollapsingMergeTree | Version-aware collapse with sign column |\n\n**Source**: `src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeTreeData.h` (lines 339\u2013351)\n\n---\n\n## 8. Replication Layer\n\nFor `ReplicatedMergeTree`, all merges and mutations are coordinated via ZooKeeper:\n- Each replica maintains a `/replicas/<name>/queue` of log entries.\n- `ReplicatedMergeTreeQueue` (`src/Storages/MergeTree/ReplicatedMergeTreeQueue.cpp`) applies entries (merges, mutations, fetches) in order.\n- `MergeFromLogEntryTask` (`src/Storages/MergeTree/MergeFromLogEntryTask.cpp`) and `MutateFromLogEntryTask` wrap `MergeTask` / `MutateTask`.\n- Part replication between replicas uses `DataPartsExchange` (`src/Storages/MergeTree/DataPartsExchange.cpp`).\n",
